    <section class="core-section-container
        core-section-container--with-border border-b-1 border-solid border-color-border-faint py-4 text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us">
<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Enqura is an AI-driven technology company that empowers institutions with innovative, secure, end-to-end digital solutions.

With our headquarters in London, we support banks, fintechs, insurance companies, telcos, and other institutions around the world on their digital transformation journey enabling them to deliver seamless and personalised services at scale. 

Our next-generation platform offers remote ID verification, strong authentication, advanced payment system &amp; open banking infrastructure, AI-powered virtual assistant, and omnichannel customer journey orchestration. 

While many institutions struggle with legacy systems, fragmented customer journeys, and the complexity of managing multiple technology vendors, Enqura bridges this gap with a unified AI-powered platform that simplifies integration, accelerates implementation, and reduces project costs.
          </p>

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Enqura Founder &amp; CEO <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/in/metinkarabiber?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Metin Karabiber</a> attended the <a class="link" href="https://ca.linkedin.com/company/finance-montreal?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Finance Montréal</a> &amp; Portage Confluence.
Together with our exclusive partner <a class="link" href="https://ca.linkedin.com/company/smartque?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SmartQue</a>, we had the opportunity to showcase our AI-driven financial technology platform, Enqura Fintech Five, to potential customers, business partners, and portfolio companies. We continue to expand our presence in North America, supporting the adoption of AI-driven financial technologies such as digital ID verification, open banking and strong &amp; passwordless authentication

🇨🇦 With our Representative Office in Canada, we are getting stronger in the region and aiming to lead the fintech sector across North America with our innovative technologies.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary"><a class="link" href="https://az.linkedin.com/company/algoritma-it?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Algoritma</a> embraces AI-Driven Digital ID Verification with EnQualify!
We are proud to welcome Algoritma as a new Enqura customer, marking another important step for EnQualify in Azerbaijan. With this agreement, Algoritma will leverage EnQualify, our award-winning digital identity verification solution, to strengthen compliance and elevate customer onboarding.

This milestone was formalized with a signing ceremony attended by Toghrul Guliyev (Chairman of the Board, Algoritma), <a class="link" href="https://az.linkedin.com/in/ziya-sadikhov-0b466953?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Ziya Sadikhov</a> (CEO, Algoritma), <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/in/metinkarabiber?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Metin Karabiber</a> (Founder &amp; CEO, Enqura), and <a class="link" href="https://az.linkedin.com/in/qadirbeyli?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Ali Qadirbeyli</a> (Country Manager, Enqura Azerbaijan).

This collaboration is not just about today, it opens the door for broader adoption of EnQualify across non-banking credit institutions in Azerbaijan. By setting a new benchmark in secure and seamless digital ID verification, EnQualify is positioned to become the market’s leading solution. Our future-ready approach ensures customers remain compliant as regulations evolve, while our collaborations mindset goes beyond contracts sharing knowledge and guidance to secure long-term success.
🔗 Learn more about EnQualify: <a class="link" href="http://www.enqura.com/enqualify?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>www.enqura.com/enqualify</a> 

-----

Algoritma, EnQualify ilə Süni İntellekt əsaslı Rəqəmsal Şəxsiyyət Doğrulamasını qəbul edir!
Biz, EnQualify-in Azərbaycandakı növbəti mühüm addımını işarələyən yeni Enqura müştərisi kimi Algoritma-nı qarşılamaqdan qürur duyuruq. Bu razılaşma ilə Algoritma, mükafat qazanmış rəqəmsal şəxsiyyət doğrulama həllimiz EnQualify-dan istifadə edərək uyğunluğu gücləndirəcək və müştəri cəlb etməni yeni səviyyəyə qaldıracaq.

Bu mərhələ, Toğrul Quliyev (Təsisçi, Algoritma), Ziya Sadıxov (Baş icraçı direktor, Algoritma), Metin Karabiber (Təsisçi və Baş icraçı direktor, Enqura) və Əli Qadirbəyli (Ölkə meneceri, Enqura Azərbaycan) tərəfindən imzalanma mərasimi ilə rəsmiləşdirildi.

Bu əməkdaşlıq yalnız bu günlə məhdudlaşmır, Azərbaycanda bank olmayan kredit təşkilatlarında EnQualify-in daha geniş tətbiqinə qapı açır. Təhlükəsiz və fasiləsiz rəqəmsal şəxsiyyət doğrulamasında yeni meyar qoyaraq, EnQualify bazarın aparıcı həllinə çevrilməyə hazırdır. Gələcəyə yönəlik yanaşmamız müştərilərin dəyişən qaydalarla uyğun qalmasını təmin edir, əməkdaşlıq fəlsəfəmiz isə müqavilələri aşaraq bilik və təcrübə paylaşmaqla uzunmüddətli uğuru təmin edir.

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">The UAE Central Bank has made a bold move: phasing out SMS OTPs by March 2026. 
Why? Because SMS OTPs are phishable, interceptable, and no longer secure enough for modern digital banking. 

That’s where EnSecure comes in. 
With passwordless authentication and built-in biometrics, EnSecure ensures compliance with UAE’s new mandate while delivering a faster, more secure, and seamless user experience. 

From built in Face ID &amp; Touch ID to secure channel, session binding, and device integrity checks, EnSecure goes far beyond outdated OTPs. 

It’s time for financial institutions to move from phishable codes to frictionless trust. 
For more information, please contact us; <a class="link" href="mailto:sales@enqura.com?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>sales@enqura.com</a> | <a class="link" href="http://www.enqura.com?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>www.enqura.com</a>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary"><a class="link" href="https://ca.linkedin.com/company/smartque?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>SmartQue</a>, the provider of secure and scalable fintech solutions and <a class="link" href="https://uk.linkedin.com/company/enqura?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Enqura</a>’s exclusive North American partner, is pleased to announce <a class="link" href="https://ca.linkedin.com/in/roykao?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Roy Kao</a> has joined the company as a Strategic Advisor. Roy is a recognized leader and advisor in Canadian financial services transformation and fintech innovation development and will guide SmartQue’s market entry and positioning, client engagement, and regulatory and industry relationship activities as we bring Enqura’s award winning solutions to support our banks, fintech, insurance, and other institutional clients on their open banking and digital transformation journeys.</p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">4 AI Models. One Mobile Device. All in Seconds, Simultaneously.
EnQualify's four specialized AI models work together in real time to stop even the most advanced presentation attacks:

✅ Replay Attack Detection
Spots anomalies like light flickers and screen patterns in video sources.
✅ Printed Attack Detection
Identifies flat, printed images with depth analysis.
✅ Mask Attack Detection (2D &amp; 3D)
Detects both simple paper masks and hyper-realistic silicone replicas.
✅ Deepfake Detection
Exposes AI-generated faces through motion and depth analysis.

All these checks run seamlessly on-device, even in low-connectivity environments, ensuring unmatched security and a smooth digital onboarding experience.

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">The more sophisticated the fraud, the smoother the experience we deliver. that’s the EnQualify difference.
At Enqura, we don’t just respond to new fraud vectors, we proactively shape the standards for digital identity security. Built on our AI on Mobile Edge technology, EnQualify enables fast, seamless, and highly secure identity verification even in low-connectivity environments.

Its liveness engine is trained to distinguish genuine human presence from synthetic attempts, offering robust protection against deepfake and spoofing attacks without compromising on speed or user experience.

✅ The result?
Fraud risk minimized. Compliance elevated. And a best-in-class customer onboarding experience that’s trusted across industries.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">The AI Revolution is Accelerating
According to a recent GlobeNewswire report, the total AI market including software,
hardware, and services is projected to reach $1.03 trillion by 2030, growing at a
staggering CAGR of 39.1% from $103 billion in 2023.

Even more striking: Generative AI alone is expected to hit $75.7 billion by 2028, up from just
$2.8 billion in 2023, a 93.7% CAGR.
📈 These numbers reflect more than just market momentum. They signal a fundamental
shift in how industries operate, innovate, and deliver value.

At Enqura, we believe that strategic innovation isn't just about keeping up, it's about
shaping what's next. This is why we continuously follow market insights like these, ensuring
our AI-driven financial technologies are not only future-ready, but also grounded in real
market needs.
